<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="performance-appraisal">Performance appraisal<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#performance-appraisal" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>This refers to evaluating an employee's current and/or past performance relative to his or her performance standards</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="performance-appraisal-tools">Performance Appraisal tools<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#performance-appraisal-tools" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Formal annual performance appraisals form</li>
<li>Probationary reviews</li>
<li>Informal one-to-one review discussions</li>
<li>Skill- or job-related tests</li>
<li>Survey of opinion of others who have dealings with the individual</li>
<li>360 degrees assessment</li>
<li>Balance score card (teams)</li>
<li>Graphic rating scale</li>
<li>Observation on the job</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="what-to-appraise">What to Appraise<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#what-to-appraise" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>⋄</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\diamond</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord">⋄</span></span></span></span></span> Assessing overall job performance
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>⋄</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\diamond</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord">⋄</span></span></span></span></span> Factors to evaluate:</p>
<ul>
<li>Technical competencies</li>
<li>Organizational Values</li>
<li>Efficiency of accomplishing work tasks</li>
<li>Observance of safety rules</li>
<li>Timeliness</li>
<li>Communication skills</li>
<li>Customer service</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="performance-appraisal-process">Performance Appraisal process<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#performance-appraisal-process" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Deciding which targets to appraise</li>
<li>Collecting the information needed to measure performance</li>
<li>Comparing results with relevant targets</li>
<li>Judging the degree to which targets were met</li>
<li>Deciding on the course of action (rewards and sanctions)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="challenges-of-conducting-performance-appraisal">Challenges of conducting Performance Appraisal<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#challenges-of-conducting-performance-appraisal" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Unclear standards because of ambiguous traits and degrees of merit</li>
<li>Halo effect—the influence of the rater’s general impression</li>
<li>Central tendency—rating all employees average</li>
<li>Leniency or strictness of supervisors</li>
<li>Bias—the tendency to allow individual differences such as personality, race, age, sex to affect ratings</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="effective-performance-appraisals">Effective performance appraisals<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#effective-performance-appraisals" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Effective performance appraisals ensure that:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>employees and supervisors learn and understand problems associated with the process</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The right tools are used</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Supervisors are trained to avoid errors of central tendency and leniency</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Outside influences are controlled</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Employee diaries are kept for objectivity and accuracy</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The use of any of these methods depends on the purpose of the appraisal</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="compensation-rewards">Compensation &amp; Rewards<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#compensation-rewards" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Compensation – Covers all rewards that individuals receive as a result of their employment and consequent expenditure of their efforts, time and energy in the organization.</p>
<p>It consists of:</p>
<p>a) Pay/base/basic pay – the money that a person receives for performing a job e.g. salary/wages.
b) Compensation – Covers all rewards that individuals receive as a result of their employment and consequent expenditure of their efforts, time and energy in the organization. It consists of:
c) a) Pay/base/basic pay – the money that a person receives for performing a job e.g. salary/wages.
d) Incentives – compensation given to employees for extra tasks, better performance or unique contribution, e.g. over time pay, commissions.
e) – These will inspire the staff to take up extra responsibilities, improve performance and have job satisfaction.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="role-of-compensation-and-rewards">Role of compensation and rewards<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#role-of-compensation-and-rewards" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>An effective workforce strategy will address the core challenges of:</p>
<ul>
<li>improving recruitment</li>
<li>improving the performance of the existing workforce</li>
<li>Slowing the rate at which workers leave the health workforce</li>
</ul>
<p>Incentives can play a role in all these areas by providing a means through which health systems can attract and retain essential and highly sought-after health care professionals</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="employee-wellness">Employee Wellness<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#employee-wellness" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>It encompasses health and safety.</p>
<p><strong>Safety</strong> – involves protecting employees from injuries caused by work related accidents or activities</p>
<p><strong>Health</strong> – employees freedom from illness; mental, physical, spiritual and their general well-being.</p>
<p>These can be achieved by providing medical cover, protective equipments, safety and health training. A state of complete physical and social wellbeing and not just the mere absence of disease.</p>
<p>It has various dimensions i.e. Social, Occupational, Spiritual, Physical, Intellectual, Emotional, Environmental Financial Mental Medical and Vocational</p>
<p>A healthy work environment is one in which there is not only absence of harmful conditions but an abundance of health promoting condition</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="wellness-can-be-assured-by-ensuring">Wellness can be assured by ensuring:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#wellness-can-be-assured-by-ensuring" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Continuous assessment of risks to health</li>
<li>Appropriate provision of information and training on health issues</li>
<li>Availability of health promoting organisational support practices</li>
<li>Effective management of occupational health and safety risks Personal security</li>
<li>Personal security</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="introduction-labour-laws">Introduction labour laws<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction-labour-laws" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Labour or employment laws are designed to protect both workers and employers</li>
<li>Labour laws are the body of laws, administrative rulings, and precedents which address the legal rights of workers and their organisations</li>
<li>The laws address issues of equal pay for equal work, discrimination, benefits e.g. insurances, pension, and others (job security)</li>
<li>Good labour laws are as good as their enforcement. Legislation is useless without law enforcement to back it up</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="some-labour-laws">Some Labour laws<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#some-labour-laws" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>There are International and national labour laws. For example in Kenya, the following are some of the labour laws</p>
<ul>
<li>The Employment Act, Cap 226</li>
<li>The Regulation of Wages and Conditions of Employment Act, Cap 229</li>
<li>The Trade Unions Act, Cap 233</li>
<li>The Trade Disputes Act, Cap 234</li>
<li>The Factories and Other Places of Work Act, Cap 514</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="employee-and-labour-relations">Employee and Labour Relations<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#employee-and-labour-relations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Employee relations covers all types of interactions among people at the work place. Its their conflict, cooperative efforts and group relationships.</p>
<p>This must be cordial to boost the morale of the workers and consequently their productivity. It also covers relations among employees themselves.</p>
<ul>
<li>Management hold the key to creating a conducive environment for such interaction to take root and flourish.</li>
<li>Labour Relations - recognition of union membership and the willingness by the management to resolve disputes through the union.</li>
<li>Employees should be given the freedom to join trade union and to participate actively and as stipulated by the Trade Unions Act and ILO.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="unit-six-commodity-and-supplies-management">UNIT SIX: COMMODITY AND SUPPLIES MANAGEMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#unit-six-commodity-and-supplies-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="purpose">Purpose:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#purpose" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The purpose of this unit is to equip the learner with knowledge and skills in managing departmental supplies.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="expected-learning-outcomes">Expected learning outcomes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#expected-learning-outcomes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Identify the roles and responsibilities of various bodies and actors in the procurement, framework and process</li>
<li>Appropriately apply the steps in procurement procedure and guide implementation of these procedures in procuring goods and services</li>
<li>Describe the Supply Chain Management including inventory and distribution management tools, disposal of stores and equipment by Public Entity</li>
<li>Identify and address challenges related to supply chain management at the workplace</li>
<li>Apply knowledge and skills to design a procurement plan for the investment / facility plan and/or priority project</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="unit-6-overview">Unit 6: overview<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#unit-6-overview" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Rationale and principles of procurement</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Procurement regulations and ethical guidelines for good procurement practices</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Roles and responsibilities of various bodies and actors in the procurement procedure</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Procurement procedures and variations at each stage based on the type of goods and services</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Procedures for contracting</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Supply Chain management tools for inventory, management, disposal of stores and equipment</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Investment plan application – designing a procurement plan for goods and services</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Challenges to supply chain management in health systems</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="current-classification-of-procurement-entities">Current classification of procurement entities<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#current-classification-of-procurement-entities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p><strong>Class A</strong> are Ministries and State Corporations</p>
<p><strong>Class B</strong> are City Councils, Universities, Judiciary, Commissions, Colleges, Cooperative Societies, Parliament, Districts, Provincial Hospitals and SAGAs</p>
<p><strong>Class C</strong> are Municipalities, County Councils, Urban Councils and Schools, District Hospitals, Sub District and Dispensaries, CDF</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="anatomy-of-kenya-s-public-procurement-and-disposal-act">Anatomy of Kenya's Public Procurement and Disposal Act<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anatomy-of-kenya-s-public-procurement-and-disposal-act" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-purpose-of-the-act">The purpose of the Act<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-purpose-of-the-act" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>To establish procedures to achieve the following objectives:</li>
<li>To maximize the economy and efficiency</li>
<li>To promote competition and ensure that the competitors are treated fairly</li>
<li>To promote the integrity and fairness of those procedures</li>
<li>To increase transparency and accountability in those procedures</li>
<li>To increase public confidence in those procedures</li>
<li>To facilitate the promotion of the local industry and economic development</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="application-of-the-regulations">Application of the Regulations.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#application-of-the-regulations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>These Regulations apply to public entities as enlisted under Section 3(1) of the ACT that is-</p>
<ul>
<li>Any body using public assets in any form of contractual undertaking.</li>
<li>Companies owned by public entity</li>
<li>Any body in which the Government has a controlling share</li>
</ul>
<p>Acquisition of goods and services not classified as procurement according to the Act</p>
<p>(Section 4(2))</p>
<ul>
<li>Retaining of services of an individual for a period of term if the individual works as though one was an employee.</li>
<li>Acquiring stores and equipment disposed by a public entity.</li>
<li>Acquiring of services provided by Government or a department of the Government.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Conflict with other Acts</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>This act prevails on matters of pro
<strong>In relation to donor funds Conflict with international agreements</strong></li>
<li>The Act prevails except in instances of negotiated grants and loans.
<strong>Conflict with Donor conditions</strong></li>
<li>Donor conditions to prevail with respect to procurement</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>BODIES AND ACTORS INVOLVED IN PROCUREMENT PROCESS: ROLES AND FUNCTIONS</strong>
<strong>Key Bodies and Actors: Membership, roles and functions</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Public Procurement Oversight Authority (PPOA)</li>
<li>Public Procurement Oversight Authority and the Director General</li>
<li>Public Procurement Oversight Advisory Board (PPOAB)</li>
<li>Public Procurement Administrative Review Board</li>
<li>Internal Organization of Public Entities</li>
<li>Procurement Unit</li>
<li>Procurement committee</li>
<li>Tendering committee</li>
<li>Roles of Heads of Departments</li>
<li>Evaluation committee</li>
<li>Inspection and acceptance committee</li>
<li>Disposal committee</li>
</ul>
<p>There ought to be separation of roles to ensure that procurement contracting process is accountable.
Within a Public Entity the procurement contracting functions should hence be separated.</p>
<p>Why?:</p>
<ul>
<li>To avoid conflicts of interest.</li>
<li>To promote the integrity and fairness of the procedures { (Sub-Section 2(c) of the Act) }</li>
<li>To increase transparency and accountability in the procedures { (Sub-Section 2 (d) of the Act) } Hence- A Public Entity shall establish a tender committee, procurement unit and other bodies required under the regulations for making procurement decisions { (Subsection26 (4)) }</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="bodies-involved-in-regulation-of-public-procurement">Bodies involved in Regulation of Public Procurement<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#bodies-involved-in-regulation-of-public-procurement" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="b5047824">Public Procurement Oversight Authority (PPOA) – Functions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#b5047824" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Monitoring the performance of the public procurement system and report to the Minister (M&amp;E)</li>
<li>Assisting in the implementation of an efficient and effective public procurement system</li>
<li>Preparation of manuals</li>
<li>Providing advice and assistance to procuring entities</li>
<li>Issuing directions to procuring entities</li>
<li>Offering other functions provided under this Act.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="promotion-of-professionalism">Promotion of Professionalism<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#promotion-of-professionalism" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>The Authority to assist in the establishment of an examination body and professional association for procurement professionals.</li>
<li>Training and professional development</li>
<li>Ensuring engagement of procurement professionals</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-director-general">The Director General<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-director-general" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>The Chief Executive of the Authority.</li>
<li>Appointed by the Advisory Board</li>
<li>Term of office – 5 years, renewable once.</li>
<li>Conditions for termination by the Advisory Boards:</li>
<li>Incompetence</li>
<li>Infirmity</li>
<li>Conviction</li>
</ul>
<p>Corruption
Employed in other public office
Bankruptcy.
Sources of Funds</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Funds of the authority</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Money appropriated by Parliament</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Loans/grants</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Revenue/fees for services rendered</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Capacity building levy</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Public Procurement Oversight Advisory Board (PPOAB)</strong>
Composition – 9 members appointed by the Minister from persons nominated by prescribed (private and public) organizations. (First schedule for prescribed organizations), and the Director-General.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Functions:</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Approve estimates of revenue and expenditures of the Authority.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Advise the Authority</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Recommend appointment or termination of Director-General in accordance with this Act.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Other functions and duties provided within the Act</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Public Procurement Administrative Review Board</strong>
Continued from the previous Public Procurement Regulations. -Legal Notice No 51 of March 2001
Composition of the Board shall be as prescribed in the regulations.
The Authority shall provide administrative services to the Review Board.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>The Internal Organization of Public Entities Relating to Procurement</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Significance of the Internal organization</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Decision making process</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>in a systematic and structured manner.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Decision making structure</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Oversight function by the Accounting officer/CEO at PE level</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Establishment of Tender Committee, Procurement Committees and Procurement Unit</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Head of Departments participation in the procurement process.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Coordination and Secretariat services offered by the Procurement Unit</p>
</li>
<li>

</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="planning">Planning<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#planning" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Planning Procurement annually within approved budgets</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="compliance-responsibilities">Compliance Responsibilities<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#compliance-responsibilities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Accounting officers to ensure that the Act is complied with</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="outsourcing-of-procurement-by-the-pe-or-by-the-authority">Outsourcing of procurement by the PE or by the Authority<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#outsourcing-of-procurement-by-the-pe-or-by-the-authority" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>To a Procuring agent who shall comply with the Act, Regulations and the Authority's circulars</li>
<li>To another Procuring Entity</li>
<li><strong>NB</strong>: Authority to register procuring agents</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-tender-committee">THE TENDER COMMITTEE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-tender-committee" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-roles-sub-section-10-2-of-the-regulations">The Roles-Sub-section 10 (2) of the Regulations<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-roles-sub-section-10-2-of-the-regulations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>To review, verify and ascertain that all procurement and disposal has been undertaken in accordance with the Act, Regulations and terms set out in the tender document.</li>
<li>To approve, select, award contracts to successful bidders where value exceeds threshold in 1st Schedule</li>
<li>To ensure availability of funds for procurement under consideration</li>
<li>To ensure intended payment not to exceed prevailing market prices</li>
<li><strong>Pre-adjudication action</strong>: Procurement Unit to carry out periodic market surveys {(Reg.8 (3) (z)}.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-tender-committee-roles">The Tender Committee: roles<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-tender-committee-roles" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Review selection of procurement method (most preferred-open tender)</li>
<li>Ensure any other procurement method is in line with the Act and Regulations.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h4 level="4" id="pre-adjudication-action">Pre-adjudication action<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#pre-adjudication-action" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h4></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Selected procurement method is to be included in the Procurement Plan (Reg.21 (1) (h) and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Complying with conditions for use of "Alternative Procurement Procedures" in Part VI of the Act.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Review and approve aggregations of procurement, packaging or use lots if proposed. Approve list of tenderers in case of restricted tendering pursuant to Reg.54 (3)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Invitation of tenders from at least 10 persons selected Sub-Reg.54 (3)(a) Fulfilling the conditions for use of Restricted Tendering Section 73 (2) of the Act.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Approve list of persons qualified to submit proposal pursuant to Section 80 of the Act
<strong>Pre-adjudication action</strong>: Examination and evaluation of Expressions of Interest to determine qualification for invitation to submit proposal</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Approve negotiation under Section 75 and 80 of the Act
<strong>Pre-adjudication action</strong>:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Negotiation is allowed in respect of Direct Procurement (Section 75 of the Act) and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>In respect of Selection of the most advantageous proposal determined with regards to Section 80 of the Act.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>NB</strong>: Requirements for negotiation should be stipulated in Bid document or of Letter of Invitation as appropriate.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Approve: Amendments of contracts previously awarded by the Tender Committee in accordance with terms and conditions in the Regulations</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Approve list of persons to be given Request for Quotation pursuant to Reg.59 (3)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Pre-adjudication action</strong>:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Selection of qualified persons from maintained list and/or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>From knowledge of the market.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>NB</strong>: Selected list of qualified persons can be supplemented by other known sources in the market</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>To review the quarterly reports on quotations that have been awarded by procurement committee.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>NB</strong>: This is in accordance with Reg 10 (2) (a) which states that Tender Committee shall review, verify that ALL procurements and disposals have been undertaken in accordance with the Act and the Regulations</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>To undertake any other functions and duties as are provided under the Regulations or as may</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>be stipulated by the Authority.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-tender-committee-composition">The Tender Committee: Composition<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-tender-committee-composition" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Established in the manner set out in Second Schedule to the Regulations to consist of:</p>
<ul>
<li>Not less than FIVE members</li>
<li>Have as its secretary, the procurement professional in charge of procurement unit
Categories of Tender committees in Second Schedule cover Procuring entities in</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-tender-committee-procedures-for-meetings">The Tender Committee: Procedures for meetings<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-tender-committee-procedures-for-meetings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>line with Section 3 of the Act- Definition of Procuring Entities</p>
<p>Tender committees membership to include <strong>alternate members</strong></p>
<p>Only alternate member to attend meetings whenever the member is unable to attend</p>
<p>Quorum to be FIVE including the Chairman</p>
<p>Decision of the Committee shall be by <strong>consensus</strong></p>
<p>In case of no consensus decision shall bMembers may be <strong>paid honoraria</strong></p>
<p>The committee shall cause to be prepared the <strong>minutes</strong> of the meetings</p>
<p>The minutes shall include:</p>
<ul>
<li>A register of attendance</li>
<li>Date of the meeting</li>
<li>List of all matters considered and decision made, reasons for rejections, clarifications, minor amendments</li>
<li>A notes regarding evaluation</li>
<li>Conflicts of interest declared and <strong>any dissenting opinion among members</strong></li>
<li>Such other records as may be necessary.</li>
</ul>
<p>e made through <strong>voting by simple majority</strong></p>
<p>Where there is a tie during voting, the Chairman shall have a <strong>second and a casting vote</strong></p>
<p>A member with interest (direct or indirect) in the matter being deliberated upon shall <strong>declare the interest</strong> and shall not participate in the deliberation</p>
<p><strong>Procedures for meetings</strong></p>
<p>Members may be paid honoraria</p>
<p>The committee shall cause to be prepared the minutes of the meetings</p>
<p>The minutes shall include:</p>
<ul>
<li>A register of attendance</li>
<li>Date of the meeting</li>
<li>List of all matters considered and decision made, reasons for rejections, clarifications, minor amendments</li>
<li>A notes regarding evaluation</li>
<li>Conflicts of interest declared and any dissenting opinion among members</li>
<li>Such other records as may be necessary.</li>
<li>Committee may also invite two more observers for contract with estimated value above Kshs 50 Million</li>
<li>At leased one observer to come from a recognized private sector organization or discipline relevant to the procurement under consideration</li>
<li>Failure of an observer to a meeting shall not nullify the procurement proceedings.</li>
</ul>
<p>The Tender Committee</p>
<p>Adjudication of evaluated bids to ensure:</p>
<ul>
<li>Compliance with product specifications</li>
<li>Delivery/Lead-Time.</li>
<li>Supplier's economic standing</li>
<li>Supplier's legal standing—whether qualified to operate as supplier/vendor of the proposed goods services or works or not.</li>
</ul>
<p>Adjudication of evaluated bids to ensure:</p>
<ul>
<li>Supplier's relevant experience</li>
<li>Supplier's technical capability to perform the proposed contract</li>
<li>Supplier's responsiveness to the tender technical requirements</li>
<li>Price for delivering the goods or rendering the services</li>
<li>Total cost</li>
</ul>
<p>Procurement Committee</p>
<p>Roles</p>
<ul>
<li>Responsible for procurement below the threshold for Tender Committee</li>
<li>May approve or reject submissions with reasons.</li>
<li>May approve submission subject to <strong>minor clarification</strong> by procurement unit</li>
<li>Shall not modify any submission or reject submission without justified reasons</li>
<li>Any rejected submission maybe resubmitted (with further clarity or details)</li>
<li>Committee to provide explanations and justifications of its decisions.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="composition">Composition<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#composition" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>An official delegated the role of being a Chairman by the Head of the Procuring Entity</li>
<li>The Finance officer or an officer carrying out related functions</li>
<li>Three members appointed by Accounting Officer</li>
<li>Secretary—an officer appointed by Head of Procurement Unit.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="procedures-for-meetings">Procedures for Meetings<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#procedures-for-meetings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p><strong>Quorum—Chairman</strong> and at least two other members</p>
<p>A member unable to attend a meeting may delegate authority to an appropriate official</p>
<p>The committee to ensure that the delegated authority is to an official with <strong>appropriate skill and experience</strong></p>
<p>Decisions of the committee shall be by consensus, otherwise the decision shall be through <strong>voting</strong> by simple majority</p>
<p>In case a of a tie in voting the Chairman’s vote shall have as second or casting vote.</p>
<ul>
<li>A member with interest (direct or indirect) in the matter being deliberated upon shall declare the interest and shall not participate in the deliberations.</li>
<li>The Committee may invite independent observer or member of procurement unit to explain submission or provide technical advices.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-procurement-committee-to-adjudicate-evaluated-bids-to-ensure">The Procurement Committee to adjudicate evaluated bids to ensure:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-procurement-committee-to-adjudicate-evaluated-bids-to-ensure" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Compliance with product specifications</li>
<li>Delivery/Lead-Time.</li>
<li>Supplier’s economic standing</li>
<li>Supplier’s legal standing—whether qualified to operate as supplier/vendor of the proposed</li>
</ul>
<p>goods services or works or not.</p>
<p>The committee shall cause to be prepared the minutes of the meetings</p>
<p>The minutes shall include:</p>
<ul>
<li>A register of attendance</li>
<li>Date of the meeting</li>
<li>List of all matters considered and decision made, reasons for rejections, clarifications, minor amendments</li>
<li>A notes regarding evaluation</li>
<li>Conflicts of interest declared and any dissenting opinion among members</li>
<li>Such other records as may be necessary.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="evaluation-committee">Evaluation Committee<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#evaluation-committee" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Established for each procurement within threshold of TC</li>
<li>May comprise separate technical &amp; Financial evaluations or Combined</li>
<li>At least 3 members recommended by Proc. &amp; appointed by CEO</li>
<li>Technical evaluation in strict adherence to compliance &amp; evaluation criteria as set out in tender docs</li>
<li>Performed with due diligence within 30 days</li>
<li>Independent evaluation by each member before sharing the ratings</li>
<li>Financial evaluation within 5 days of completion of technical evaluation</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="inspection-acceptance-committee">Inspection &amp; Acceptance Committee<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#inspection-acceptance-committee" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Composed of 3 members recommended by Proc. &amp; appointed by CEO Shall:</li>
<li>inspect &amp; test goods received</li>
<li>ensure compliance with terms &amp; conditions of contract</li>
<li>accept or reject the deliveries</li>
<li>ensure correct quantity is received</li>
<li>goods meet technical stds</li>
<li>timely deliveries or note the delays</li>
<li>all manuals are received</li>
<li>issue interim or completion certs or GRNs</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="measures-for-redressing-grievances">MEASURES FOR REDRESSING GRIEVANCES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#measures-for-redressing-grievances" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="appeal-right">Appeal Right<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#appeal-right" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>To redress meritorious grievances of candidates and correct system failures.</p>
<p>An Administrative Review Board may grand or recommend the following remedies:</p>
<ul>
<li>Declare the legal rule or principle that govern the subject matter</li>
<li>Prohibit the procuring entity from acting or deciding unlawful</li>
<li>Annul in whole or part an unlawful act or decision of a procuring entity.</li>
<li>Revise an unlawful decision or substitute it with its own decision</li>
<li>Administrative Review Board may grand or recommend the following remedies:</li>
<li>Order that the procurement proceedings be terminated</li>
<li>Review Board to make decision in stipulated timeframe.</li>
<li>The decision to be final unless successfully reviewed by court.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="disposal-of-stores-and-equipment">Disposal of Stores and Equipment<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disposal-of-stores-and-equipment" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>What to be disposed of.</p>
<ul>
<li>Stores and Equipment that are:</li>
<li>unserviceable, obsolete or surplus</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="disposal-methods">Disposal methods<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disposal-methods" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>As recommended by Disposal Committee subject to technical report</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="disposal-committee">Disposal Committee<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disposal-committee" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>To be established in accordance with the regulations</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="disposal-methods">Disposal Methods<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disposal-methods" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>transfer to another entity</li>
<li>sale by public tender</li>
<li>sale by public auction</li>
<li>destruction, dumping or burying</li>
<li>trade-in</li>
</ul>
<p>There shall be a time limit for acceptance of recommendations of disposal committee by the</p>
<p>Accounting Officer.</p>
<p>Restriction on disposal to employees unless as prescribed in the regulations.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="managing-stores">MANAGING STORES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#managing-stores" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Items stored include:</p>
<p>a) Consumables – used within a short time (cotton wool, sutures, syringes etc)
b) Non-consumables – permanent and can be used for years</p>
<p>Procedure for equipment: deciding what to buy, ordering equipment, storing (recording, labeling and holding), issuing, controlling, maintaining and repairing</p>
<p>Store Management = Avail goods and equipment - in time - at the right place - at minimal costs</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20260119-982c40e5.jpeg" alt="img-6.jpeg"></p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20260119-f35a5034.jpeg" alt="img-7.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="stores-management-cycle-strategic-planning-3-4">Stores Management Cycle Strategic Planning 3/4<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stores-management-cycle-strategic-planning-3-4" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Strategic decisions on principles:</p>
<ul>
<li>Stock levels policy</li>
<li>Stock storage system (Centralisation level)</li>
<li>Registration system</li>
<li>What finance is needed/available?</li>
<li>Stock validation method (e.g. at cost price, depreciated, etc.)</li>
<li>Outsourcing or in-house</li>
<li>Institutional organisation</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="stores-management-cycle-strategic-planning-3-4">Stores Management Cycle Strategic Planning 3/4<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stores-management-cycle-strategic-planning-3-4" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Based on an assessment of:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>What goods and/or equipment are needed?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Legal and regulatory requirements</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>How does stores impact performance? How measured?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Organisation set-up</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Human resource requirements</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Risks and costs</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>In-house or outsourced?</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="stores-management-cycle-strategic-planning-4-4">Stores Management Cycle Strategic Planning 4/4<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stores-management-cycle-strategic-planning-4-4" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="stores-design">Stores design<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stores-design" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="decide-location-s">Decide location(s)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#decide-location-s" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Based on type stock (cold, size, climate, hazardous, sensitive)</li>
<li>When needed and where?</li>
<li>Legal and regulatory requirements</li>
<li>Access</li>
<li>Security and safety (hazardous goods, fire, accident, health)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="decide-storage-stockyard-lay-out-equipment">Decide Storage/stockyard lay-out &amp; equipment<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#decide-storage-stockyard-lay-out-equipment" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Legal and regulatory requirements</li>
<li>Conditions for storing goods and equipment</li>
<li>Access and efficiency of movement</li>
<li>Energy supply - emergency back-up needed?</li>
<li>Security measures to be installed</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="human-resource-management">Human Resource Management<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#human-resource-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Detailed organogram and job descriptions</li>
<li>Recruit and manage staff (Number, qualifications, motivation, training, supervision, monitoring)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="unit-seven-public-relations-and-customer-care">UNIT SEVEN: PUBLIC RELATIONS AND CUSTOMER CARE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#unit-seven-public-relations-and-customer-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="purpose">Purpose:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#purpose" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The purpose of this unit is to equip the learner with knowledge and skills in managing the public</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="expected-learning-outcomes">Expected learning outcomes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#expected-learning-outcomes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>By the end of the session the learners shall be able to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Describe the nature of customers in Health Systems</li>
<li>Discuss why we need Customer Relationship Management (CRM)</li>
<li>Explain the expectations, wants and needs of the customers in Health Systems</li>
</ul>
<p>Customer Relationship Management (CRM) is a social process of managing all networks of communication to ensure mutual understanding between the service provider (health worker) and the customer (e.g. patient from OPD or Nurse in the Theatre).</p>
<p>Relationships are preceded by social communication for both internal and External Customers. Communication in this context relates to both verbal and nonverbal. In order to achieve effective communication there is a need to ensure the existence of the ‘integrated marketing system’ (Triangular model).</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="triangular-model">Triangular Model<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#triangular-model" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20260119-e77c7a6f.jpeg" alt="img-8.jpeg"></p>
<p>Integrated System Interactive Marketing +ve or -ve (EMPLOYEES) (EXT. CUSTOMERS) (ORGANISATION) HIGH PERFORMANCE</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-customers-in-health-system">The Customers in Health System<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-customers-in-health-system" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The customers in health systems can be categorized as internal customer and external customers.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="internal-customers">Internal Customers<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#internal-customers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Internal customers include all individuals, departments, sections within the organization who</p>
<p>use the output of your job (e.g. Pharmacist &amp; the Accountant of the Hospital). The satisfaction of the internal customers is crucial to the achievement of the organizational goals and positive image. Internal customer relationship is a crucial part of CRM as when it fails it gives room for Gossip that distorts the image of the organization.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="external-customers">External Customers<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#external-customers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>External customers include individuals, organizations and anybody outside the organization who buy/use/ the goods and services provided by the organization. In the case of Health service; suppliers, patients, regulatory bodies and the like form the external customers.</p>
<p>The concept of Integrated Marketing targets the employees, employers &amp; external Customers given that it highlights the roles of each of the above mentioned. It is important to note that a customer may belong to various categories.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="categories-of-customers">Categories of Customers<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#categories-of-customers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Internal Vs External</li>
<li>Industrial Vs Individual</li>
<li>Existing Vs New</li>
<li>Physical Product Customers Vs Service Customers</li>
<li>Short term Vs Long term</li>
<li>General Vs Prestigious (VIP)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="types-of-customers-in-the-individual-markets-human-human-interaction">Types of customers in the individual markets (human-human interaction)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#types-of-customers-in-the-individual-markets-human-human-interaction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-silent-uncommunicative-customer">The silent (uncommunicative) Customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-silent-uncommunicative-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Is shy, quiet or deliberately uncommunicative; scarcely talks (e.g. a patient with an STD)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-talkative-customer">The talkative Customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-talkative-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Is friendly and has a sense of humor, willing to talk about different issues</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-sarcastic-over-familiar-customer">The sarcastic (over-familiar) Customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-sarcastic-over-familiar-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Talks a lot; often fast, without stop, could be the most difficult customer (e.g. a doctor who is a patient)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-good-nurtured-customer">The good-nurtured Customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-good-nurtured-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Says yes to almost everything but will not make a decision (e.g. a Nurse who fears a doctor or a doctor with his boss</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="the-angry-bad-tempered-customer">The angry-bad tempered Customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-angry-bad-tempered-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Is irritated with something small (trivial)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-hostile-rude-argumentative-customer">The hostile, rude, argumentative Customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-hostile-rude-argumentative-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Very difficult customer; she/he always attacks you on whatever you say to challenge your position (a Pharmacist when procuring the drugs)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-aloof-disinterested-customer">The aloof/disinterested customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-aloof-disinterested-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Similar to the silent customers, very reserved.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-busy-customer-impulse-customer">The busy Customer (Impulse Customer)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-busy-customer-impulse-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Appears busy, has hurried movements and air of anxiety and can't concentrate on service offered at the counter.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-invisible-customer-telephone-customer">The invisible Customer/Telephone Customer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-invisible-customer-telephone-customer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
